+<h2 id="h-ilicet-sata-edax-artesque-submersum-amicitur-ad" tabindex="-1"><a class="direct-link" href="#h-ilicet-sata-edax-artesque-submersum-amicitur-ad" aria-hidden="true">#</a> Ilicet sata edax artesque submersum amicitur ad</h2>
 <p>Et <a href="#misit-aures">oculis</a> vadit flavusque. Responsa sceleris ibat nitentem Crenaee mors pendens inquit moriemur artem armos praeter illud, Aloidas olorinis seque et?</p>
 <blockquote>
 <p>Territa qui nostro, magis palus erat, hoc <a href="#coniunx-et">solem</a>. Fronti triumphos vinaque; vultusque tollere raptatur Iuppiter, tibi fatalis in modo quotiens minimamque et Minyae. Dantem optabile <em>aurum</em>; videt est ponit se vultu fervet superi, sub segnior placidique Tremorque. Fictilibus ignis; oris esse cum huius <a href="#me-eratque">ultoris</a>, terrae Delphica.</p>

diff --git a/src/utils/filters.js b/src/utils/filters.js
@@ -0,0 +1,12 @@
+const { DateTime } = require("luxon");
+
+module.exports = {
+  postDate: function (dateObj) {
+    return DateTime.fromJSDate(dateObj).toLocaleString(DateTime.DATE_MED);
+  },
+
+  w3Date: function (value) {
+    const dateObject = new Date(value);
+    return dateObject.toLocaleDateString();
+  },
+};
diff --git a/src/utils/markdown.js b/src/utils/markdown.js
@@ -0,0 +1,32 @@
+const markdownIt = require("markdown-it");
+const markdownItAnchor = require("markdown-it-anchor");
+
+const anchorSlugify = (s) =>
+  encodeURIComponent(
+    "h-" +
+      String(s)
+        .trim()
+        .toLowerCase()
+        .replace(/[.,\/#!$%\^&\*;:{}=_`~()]/g, "")
+        .replace(/\s+/g, "-")
+  );
+
+const markdown = markdownIt({
+  html: true,
+  breaks: true,
+  typographer: true,
+  linkify: true,
+}).use(markdownItAnchor, {
+  permalink: markdownItAnchor.permalink.ariaHidden({
+    placement: "before",
+    class: "direct-link",
+    symbol: "#",
+    level: [1, 2, 3, 4],
+  }),
+  permalinkBefore: true,
+  permalinkAttrs: () => ({ "aria-hidden": true }),
+  level: 2,
+  slugify: anchorSlugify,
+});
+
+module.exports = markdown;
